<script type="text/javascript" src="/public/js/jquery-3.1.1.js;jsessionid=mFArRnSDXjHF25b4c+ITZSog"></script>

<script>

$(document).ready(function($){   
	
	// This constant is used to decide when the next batch of vacancies should be painted while user scrolls down VBFA. 
	// When user reaches this percent of document height when scrolling down, next batch of vacancies will be printed.
	var SCROLL_TRIGGER_PERCENTAGE = 90; 
	
	//DOM Ready call contact us popup function
	
	//global variable to hold location list
	window.globalLocationList = null;
	
	// Global variable to maintain the search result; this gets updated whenever a search is done
	// This is used to pass into loadMoreVacancies(...). In it, it is treated as the source from which the next batch of vacancies are to be printed
	// This is initialised to window.vacancyCollection here (at page load) as no-filtering has happened until now, i.e. searchResult equals all vacancies
	// window.vacancyCollection is declared & initialised by code in vacancyDetails.jsp
	window.searchResult = window.vacancyCollection;
	
	// global variable to hold the vacTile design
	window.vacTileDesign = null;
		
	initVacTileTooltips(); //Vacancy tooltip function invocation 

	offTouchJobLink(); // calling offTouchJobLink() to disable the clickability of the job position and company name 
	/*
	The below function extract the href from job position link and explicitly open that link in a new tab when click on vactile(.job_content). 
	Function is only works for touch devices - CC4627
	*/
    $(".job-content").on("click", function() { // click event on the job-content  
    if('ontouchstart' in window)//ontouchstart - The event occurs when a finger is placed on a touch screen
	{
      var jobLink = $(this).find('.job-link').attr('href');// get the href form the .job-link class
      window.open(jobLink, '_blank').focus(); // open the href in a new tab and focus to it
	}
    });
	
	// Live search controller
   	$('.live-search-list').each(function(){ // select div in live-search-list block
   		
   		var vacTitle = $(this).find('.job-link').text();
   		var vacRefNo = $(this).find('.job-ref-value').text();
   		var vacJobOwner = $(this).find('.job-owner').text();
   		var allTextInItem = vacTitle + ' ' + vacRefNo + ' ' + vacJobOwner;
   		
   		$(this).attr('data-search-term', allTextInItem.toLowerCase()); // convert all text into lowercase and assign to data-search-term attribute
   		
   	});
   	
   	// Construct drop-down menu of the location search box
   	constructLocationDropdownList();
   	
   	//added bottom padding if vacancies less than the screen size
	$('.live-search-box').on('focusout', function(){
		if($(".vbfa-screen-holder").innerHeight() <= screenHeight/2){
			$(".vbfa-screen-holder .vbfa-screen").css({ 'padding-bottom' : '2%'});
		}else
			$(".vbfa-screen-holder .vbfa-screen").css({ 'padding-bottom' : '2%'});
	});
   	
   	$('.live-search-box').on('keyup', function(){ // function call on key release event 
   	 $('[data-toggle="tooltip"]').tooltip('hide');//hide the tooltip when keyword search
		// Retrieve vacancy collection in window scope; window.vacancyCollection is declared & initialised by code in vacancyDetails.jsp
		var vacancies = window.vacancyCollection;
		
   		filter(vacancies);
   	}); // End live search controller 

   	
   	/* added to load locations list without third party liberaries */
   $('button.btn.btn-primary').on('click', function(){
	   constructLocationDropdownList();
   });	
   	
   	
   	//Event handler for mouse click on close button 
   $('.location-dropdown .close-button').on('click', function(){
	   $('input.location-search-box').val('');
	   $('input.location-search-box').focus();
	   $('.location-dropdown .dropdown-toggle.btn.btn-primary').show();
	   $('.location-dropdown .close-button').hide();
	   
	   // Retrieve vacancy collection in window scope; window.vacancyCollection is declared & initialised by code in vacancyDetails.jsp
	   var vacancies = window.vacancyCollection;
	   
	   filter(vacancies);
   });
   
   	/* get matching location list when user types the location */
   $('input.location-search-box').on('keyup', function(){
	   
	   //hide close button and show dropdown button
	   $('.location-dropdown .dropdown-toggle.btn.btn-primary').show();
	   $('.location-dropdown .close-button').hide();
	   
	   	var locationSearchBox = $(this);
  		var locationSearchValue = locationSearchBox.val().toLowerCase().trim();
  		
  		var locationList = window.globalLocationList;
  		var autoCompleteLocations = new Array();
  		
  		if(locationList !== null){
  			$.each(locationList, function(index, value){
  				var locationItem = value.toLowerCase();
  				
  				if(locationItem.indexOf(locationSearchValue) !== -1){
  					autoCompleteLocations.push(value);
  				}
  			});
  		}
  		
  		createDropDownMenu(autoCompleteLocations);	
  		$('.location-dropdown').addClass('open');
  		$('button.dropdown-toggle.btn.btn-primary').attr('aria-expanded',true);
 		
   });	
   	
	//added bottom padding if vacancies less than the screen size
	$('input.location-search-box').on('focusout', function(){
		if($(".vbfa-screen-holder").innerHeight() <= screenHeight/2){
			$(".vbfa-screen-holder .vbfa-screen").css({ 'padding-bottom' : '20%'});
		}else
			$(".vbfa-screen-holder .vbfa-screen").css({ 'padding-bottom' : '5%'});
	});

	/*
	 * handle keyboard events to navigate between the dropdown list and the location search input box 
	 * Help user to naviage in between dropdown list and the location serch input box using the keybord 
	 **/
	   $(document).keydown(function(e){
		   
		   var targetInput = $('input.location-search-box');
		  
		   /*
		   	* handles keypress events when the location search input box 
		   	* is the active element.
		    **/
		   if(targetInput.is(document.activeElement)) {
			   
			   //switch currnet event's keycode
			   switch (e.keyCode) {
			   
		        case 8://backspace key
		        //keep focus in locatin search box
		        	$('input.location-search-box').focus();
		            break;
		            
		        case 38:// up key
		        //select the last list item in the location dropdown list
			   		$('.dropdown-menu').find("li").last().children().focus();
		            break;
		            
		        case 40://down key
		        //selects the first element of the dropdown list
			   		$('.dropdown-menu').find("li").first().children().focus();
		            break;
		            
		        case 9://tab key
		        //tab key is identified as an enter in this scenario. Therefore it requires to match 
		        // location search box value with current location list and filter vacancies if needed
		        	matchLocationSearchKeyword();
		       		break;
		       		
		        case 13://entert key
		        //calls method to macht and filter vacancies. After the location match, remove focus from location search box
  		        	matchLocationSearchKeyword();
  		        	$('input.location-search-box').blur();
  		       		break;	
  		       		
		       	default:
		       		break;
		    }
		   }
		   
		   // if dropdown is expanded handle keyboard events	
		   var dropdownList = $('.dropdown.location-dropdown');
		   if(dropdownList.hasClass("open")) {
			   		   
			   switch (e.keyCode) {
		        case 38:// up key
			   		$('.dropdown-menu').find("li").last().children().focus();
		            break;
		        case 40://down key
			   		$('.dropdown-menu').find("li").first().children().focus();
		            break;
		        case 13://enter key
		        
		        /*
		        * location text value given by the user might not have the complete value. It can be
		        * only a part of the location name used to help filter out the location list.
		        * Therefore on enter keypress, identify user focused location item and 
		        * get the selected text to filter vacancies and display in the location search input box
		        */
		        	var selectedElement = $(document.activeElement);
		        	var selectedValue  = selectedElement.text();
		       	 	if(selectedValue !== null || selectedValue !== undefined){	
		       	 		
		       	 		//pass the complete name of the selected location name
		        		$('input.location-search-box').val(selectedValue);
		        		matchLocationSearchKeyword();
		        		$('input.location-search-box').blur();
		        		
		        	}
		        	
		       		break;
		    	default:
		    		$('input.location-search-box').focus();	
		    }
			   
		   }

		});
	
	 	// Bind event to trigger when focusing out of the location-search-box; 
	   	// this will trigger filtering functions only if the element that location-search-box looses focus to is a drop-down menu-item and location-search-box value is not null  
	   	$('input.location-search-box').focusout(function(e){
			var locationDropDownMenuItems = $('ul.dropdown-menu > li > a');
		   
		    var locationSearchText = $('input.location-search-box').val();
		    if (!$(e.relatedTarget).is(locationDropDownMenuItems)) {
		   		if(locationSearchText != null){
	 				matchLocationSearchKeyword(); 
		 		} 
		   	}	
		    
		    // Remove any tool-tip elements that may be open
		    $('div.tooltip').remove();
	   	});
	
   	// function used to match location search keyword value with the location list
    function matchLocationSearchKeyword(){
   		var locationSearchBox = $('input.location-search-box').val();
   		var locationSearchValue = locationSearchBox.trim();
		
   		
 	  	var locationOptions = window.globalLocationList;
   		var doesMatch = false;
   		
   		if (locationSearchValue.toLowerCase() === "All Locations".toLowerCase()) {
			doesMatch = true;
		}else{
	   		$.each(locationOptions, function(index, value){
				if (locationSearchValue.toLowerCase() === value.toLowerCase()) {
					doesMatch = true;
				}
	   		});
		}

   	   		// On focus-out, if the entered value does not match any of the items in the drop-down menu, 
   	   		// then clear the entered value before filtering vacancies
   			if (doesMatch) {
   				$('input.location-search-box').val(locationSearchValue);
   			   //hide close button and show dropdown button
   			   $('.location-dropdown .dropdown-toggle.btn.btn-primary').hide();
   			   $('.location-dropdown .close-button').show();
   			} else {
   				$('input.location-search-box').val('');
   			}
   	   		
   	   		//close dropdown list
   			$('.location-dropdown').removeClass('open');
   	  		$('button.dropdown-toggle.btn.btn-primary').attr('aria-expanded',false);
   		   
   		   	// Retrieve vacancy collection in window scope; window.vacancyCollection is declared & initialised by code in vacancyDetails.jsp
   		   	var vacancies = window.vacancyCollection;
   		   	
		   	filter(vacancies);
   	}    	
  	
    setDateLabel($('.live-search-list').find('.closing-date'));
   	
   	

	var keyWordSearchString = $('input.live-search-box').val(); 
	// Does keyWordSearchString contain a valid value at document.load (before user has ever got the chance to interact with the page)?  
	if (keyWordSearchString != undefined && keyWordSearchString != null && keyWordSearchString.length > 0) {
		// Yes means VBFA has loaded as result of a search-attempt; filtering has to be done
		
		$('input.live-search-box').val(keyWordSearchString.replace(/^0+/, ''));		
		
		// Retrieve vacancy collection in window scope; window.vacancyCollection is declared & initialised by code in vacancyDetails.jsp
		var vacancies = window.vacancyCollection;
		
		// Filter
		filter(vacancies);
	}
	
		
	// Bind handler loadMoreVacancies() to scroll event of window object so it is called when the user scrolls down, 
	// given that user has reached a certian point height-wise
	$(window).scroll(function() {
		// See if the current focus is at the preferred percentage of document height that is indicated by SCROLL_TRIGGER_PERCENTAGE (e.g. (height / 100) * 90)
	   if($(window).scrollTop() + $(window).height() > ($(document).height() / 100 * SCROLL_TRIGGER_PERCENTAGE)) {
		   // User has scrolled past height-threshold of SCROLL_TRIGGER_PERCENTAGE; paint the next batch of vacancies
		   
			// Retrieve whatever the content currently in window.searchResult. 
			// window.searchResult is initialised to window.vacancyCollection at page-load, but then updated every time user conducts a search
			var vacancies = window.searchResult;
			
			// Load the next batch of vacancies
			loadMoreVacancies(vacancies);
	   }
	});
	
	//color rows for existing vacancies in grid view. CC4732
	displayShadeRow();
   	
});

/**
 * Disabling the touch capability of the job position and company name - CC4627
 */
function offTouchJobLink(){
	// disable the touch events for company name on touch devices
	if('ontouchstart' in window)//ontouchstart - The event occurs when a finger is placed on a touch screen
	{
		$('.lbl-job-owner').css('pointer-events','none'); // changing pointer events to none 
		$('.job-link').css('pointer-events','none'); // changing pointer events to none 
	}
	}

	// This function constructs the drop-down list of the location-search-combo-box both initially at (document load) and subsequently when 
	// result vac-tiles are updated (upon being narrowed down by filtering)
	function constructLocationDropdownList() {
		//Declaring an array to hold the location list taken from the job location div.
		var locationList = new Array();
		
		if (window.vacancyCollection != undefined && window.vacancyCollection != null) {
			var vacancyCollection = window.searchResult;
			
			$.each(vacancyCollection, function(vacIndex, vacancy) {
				var vacLocations = vacancy.jobLocationsArray;
				
				if (vacLocations != undefined && vacLocations != null && vacLocations.length > 0) {
					$.each(vacLocations, function(locIndex, vacLocation) {
						if (vacLocation != undefined && vacLocation != null && vacLocation.trim().length > 0) {
							locationList.push(vacLocation);
						}
					});
				}
			});
			
		} else {
			var locationsOfVisibleVacs = $('div.live-search-list:visible').find('label.job-location');

			locationsOfVisibleVacs.each(function() { //Taking all the values belongs to the job location details div.
				var locations = $(this).find(
						'span.sub-location-tooltip span.sub-location');
				var location = '';
		
				if (locations.length > 0) { //This vac-tile contains multiple locations
					locations.each(function() {
						location = $(this).text();
						locationList.push(location);
					});
				} else { // This vac-tile contains only a single location
					location = $(this).text().trim();
					locationList.push(location);
				}
			});
		}

		//Remove duplicated from the selected values, if there are any.
		locationList = locationList.filter(function(elem, index, self) {
			return index == self.indexOf(elem);
		});

		// Sort the locationList alphabetically 
		locationList.sort();
		window.globalLocationList = locationList;

		// create drop down menu
		createDropDownMenu(locationList);

	}

	// This function creates the drop down menu and append it to the drop down list
	function createDropDownMenu(locationList) {

		$('.location-dropdown').find('ul').remove();
		var listElement = '';
		listElement += '<ul class="dropdown-menu">';
		listElement += '<li value="All Locations"><a href="#" class="location-anchor">All Locations</a></li>';

		//Apend each location to the location list dropdown 
		$
				.each(
						locationList,
						function(index, value) {
							listElement += '<li value="'+ value+'"> <a href="#" class="location-anchor">'
									+ value + '</a></li>';
						});
		listElement += '</ul>';
		$('.location-dropdown').append(listElement);

		//handles event when user selects a location element from the drop dowm list
		$('ul.dropdown-menu li').on("click", function() {

			//get the existing location search input value
			var oldLocation = $('input.location-search-box').val();

			//get selectd location name from the dropdown list
			var selectedLocation = $(this).attr('value');

			//check if the selected location is changed
			if (oldLocation !== selectedLocation) {

				//update old location value to new selected location name
				$('input.location-search-box').val(selectedLocation);
				
				// Retrieve vacancy collection in window scope; window.vacancyCollection is declared & initialised by code in vacancyDetails.jsp
				var vacancies = window.vacancyCollection; 
				
				//filter vacancies
				filter(vacancies);
			}

			//hides dropdown icon and shows close button in locatin search input box
			$('.location-dropdown .dropdown-toggle.btn.btn-primary').hide();
			$('.location-dropdown .close-button').show();

			//send focus after the faCategory area to avoid filtered vacancies from hiding on small screens 
			$('body').animate({
				scrollTop : $('#pagination').position().top
			}, 500);
		});

	}

	// This function undertakes the filtering of vacancies based both on the values in keyword search box as well as location search box
	function filterVacancies() {
		var keyWordSearchString = $('.live-search-box').val().toLowerCase(); // initialize searchTerm variable 
		var locationSearchString = $('input.location-search-box').val()
				.toLowerCase();

		if (locationSearchString === 'all locations') { // If drop-down item 'All Locations' is what is currently selected then the it will be 
			// treated as an empty value (location-based search will be bypassed in the search algorithm)
			locationSearchString = '';
		}

		var shownCount = 0;
		
		if (keyWordSearchString.length > 0) {
			if (locationSearchString.length > 0) {
				$('.live-search-list')
						.each(
								function() { // select div in live-search-list block
									var currentVacTile = $(this);
									if ($(this)
											.filter(
													'[data-search-term *= '
															+ keyWordSearchString
															+ ']').length > 0) { // check conditions and fiter matching terms
										var subLocToolTips = $(this).find(
												'span.sub-location-tooltip');
										if (subLocToolTips.length > 0) { // Tool-tip exists; indicates presence of multiple locations
											var subLocations = $(
													subLocToolTips.get(0))
													.find('span.sub-location');
											if (subLocations.length > 0) {
												var doesMatch = false;
												subLocations
														.each(function() {
															var loc = $(this)
																	.text()
																	.toLowerCase();
															if (loc === locationSearchString) {
																doesMatch = true;
																return false;
															}
														});
												if (doesMatch) {
													currentVacTile.show(); 
													updateIndex(currentVacTile, ++shownCount);
												} else {
													currentVacTile.hide();
													removeIndex(currentVacTile);
												}
											} else {
												currentVacTile.hide();
												removeIndex(currentVacTile);

											}
											return true;
										} else { // No tool-tip exists; only one location for this vac-tile
											var locTextInVacTile = $(
													$(this)
															.find(
																	'label.job-location')
															.get(0)).text()
													.trim().toLowerCase();
											if (locTextInVacTile.length > 0) {
												if (locTextInVacTile === locationSearchString) {
													currentVacTile.show();
													updateIndex(currentVacTile, ++shownCount);
												} else {
													currentVacTile.hide();
													removeIndex(currentVacTile);
												}
											} else {
												currentVacTile.hide();
												removeIndex(currentVacTile);
											}
											return true;
										}
									} else {
										currentVacTile.hide();
										removeIndex(currentVacTile);
										return true;
									}
								});
			} else { // Location search box is empty; filter only by keyword search value
				$('.live-search-list')
						.each(
								function() { // select div in live-search-list block
									if ($(this)
											.filter(
													'[data-search-term *= '
															+ keyWordSearchString
															+ ']').length > 0) { // check conditions and fiter matching terms 
										$(this).show(); // show only matched results boxes  
										updateIndex($(this), ++shownCount);
									} else {
										$(this).hide(); // hide unmatched results boxes
										removeIndex($(this));
									}
								});
			}
		} else { // Keyword search box is empty; search only by value in location search box
			if (locationSearchString.length > 0) {
				$('.live-search-list')
						.each(
								function() { // select div in live-search-list block
									var currentVacTile = $(this);
									var subLocToolTips = $(this).find(
											'span.sub-location-tooltip');
									if (subLocToolTips.length > 0) { // Tool-tip exists; indicates presence of multiple locations
										var subLocations = $(
												subLocToolTips.get(0)).find(
												'span.sub-location');
										if (subLocations.length > 0) {
											var doesMatch = false;
											subLocations
													.each(function() {
														var loc = $(this)
																.text()
																.toLowerCase();
														if (loc === locationSearchString) {
															doesMatch = true;
															return false;
														}
													});
											if (doesMatch) {
												currentVacTile.show();
												updateIndex(currentVacTile, ++shownCount);
											} else {
												currentVacTile.hide();
												removeIndex(currentVacTile);
											}
										} else {
											currentVacTile.hide();
											removeIndex(currentVacTile);
										}
										return true;
									} else { // No tool-tip exists; only one location for this vac-tile
										var locTextInVacTile = $(
												$(this).find(
														'label.job-location')
														.get(0)).text().trim()
												.toLowerCase();
										;
										if (locTextInVacTile.length > 0) {
											if (locTextInVacTile === locationSearchString) {
												currentVacTile.show();
												updateIndex(currentVacTile, ++shownCount);
											} else {
												currentVacTile.hide();
												removeIndex(currentVacTile);
											}
										} else {
											currentVacTile.hide();
											removeIndex(currentVacTile);
										}
										return true;
									}
								});
			} else { // Location search box is also empty; do no filtering, i.e. show all vac-tiles
				$('.live-search-list').each(function() { // Loop through vac-tiles 
					$(this).show(); // Show the current vac-tile
					updateIndex($(this), ++shownCount); // Update indexof the current vac-tile
				});
			}
		}

		constructLocationDropdownList();

		// Retrieve vacancy collection in window scope; window.vacancyCollection is declared & initialised by code in vacancyDetails.jsp
		var vacancies = window.vacancyCollection;

		// Retrieve whatever the content currently in window.searchResult 
		var searchResult = window.searchResult;		

		// Update the job-count displayed on VBFA to match the number now shown after being filtered
		displayJobCount(vacancies, searchResult);	
	}	
	
	/**
	 * This adjusts the "index" of the vac-tile passed in the vacTile param. 
	 * Index of a vac-tile indicates its position in the set of vac-tiles. There are two places in a vac-tile where it is used: 
	 * 1) data-index attribute of the anchor tag that is the vacancy-link  
	 * 2) index query-string parameter of the URL assigned to href of the vacancy-link (anchor tag)
	 * 
	 * "index" query-string param and "data-index" attribute are used by SAV (Standalone AdView) when correctly loading the Next/Previous vacancy from there.
	 * Therefore, when filering happens (i.e. vac-tiles get hidden/shown) values for these items must be correctly updated, for the correct functionality of SAV Next/Previous. 
	 *
	 * @param vacTile - a jQuery object wrapping a DOM element that is a vac-tile
	 * @param index - an integer that represents the index to set for the job-link of this vac-tile
	 */
	function updateIndex(vacTile, index) {
		var SERVER_PATH = '/vacancy?';
		var RID_PG = '&rid=0&pg=applicant/vacancyDetails.jsp';
		var IDX_PREFIX = 'jobAd';
		
		// Add data-index attrib if not already there
		var link = vacTile.find('a.job-link'); // Get the job-link from the vac-tile
		link.attr('data-index', IDX_PREFIX + index); // Update value of data-index attribute
		
		// Get necessary data from the vac-tile to re-compose href of its job-link with the updated index
		var ac = 'ac=' + link.attr('data-agentcode');
		var jc = '&jc=' + link.attr('id');
		var ec = '&ec=' + link.attr('data-empcode');
		var idx = '&index=' + index;
		
		// Compose new URL with updated "index" qstring param
		var url = SERVER_PATH + ac + jc + ec + idx + RID_PG;
		
		// Set new URL to link's href
		link.attr('href', url);
	}
	
	/**
	 * This removes the "data-index" attribute from job-link (anchor tag) in the vac-tile represented by vacTile parameter. 
	 * "data-index" is used by SAV, which may load after clicking on a job-link, to find the next/previous vac-tile relative to the vac-tile whose link was clicked. 
	 * If a vac-tile that is made hidden after a filtering on the page still has the data-index with the value that it had before filtering was done, this could 
	 * make SAV Next/Previous operations select the incorrect vacancy. Therefore, this function may be called on a vac-tile hidden during a filtering. 
	 * 
	 * @param vacTile - a jQuery object wrapping a DOM element that is the vac-tile whose data-index attribute needs to be removed
	 *
	 */
	function removeIndex(vacTile) {
		vacTile.find('a.job-link').removeAttr('data-index'); // Get the job-link from the vac-tile, and remove its data-index
	}
	
	
	/**
	 * This function filters vacancies on the array accpeted for "vacancies" parameter, based on value in "keyword" parameter 
	 * 
	 * This creates a search-target text for each element in "vacancies" to be compared with value for "keyword", and removes any element from "vacancies" that does not match.  
	 * The search-target is made by concatenating vacancy-title, job-spec-code and employer name properties (all lowercase) of vacancy-object in each element in "vacancies" parameter. 
	 *
	 * For example, if, 
	 *
	 * vacancy-title (joPosition) = Technical Writer
	 * job-spec-code (joCode) = 430682
	 * employer name (joEmployerName) = Some company
	 * 
	 * then search-target for this vac-tile will be: "technical writer 430682 some company"
	 *
	 * @param vacancies: An array containing vacancy-objects that is searched through to find matches
	 * @param keyword: Value to search by in "vacancies" array
	 * 
	 * @return An array of vacancy-objects representing the search result
	 */
	function filterByKeyword(vacancies, keyword) {
		// Convert keyword into lowercase
		keyword = keyword.toLowerCase();

		// If keyword is not empty
		if (keyword.length > 0) {
			// Loop through array
			// Iterating in reverse order due to objects' indexes being modified as matching elements get removed
			// When looping from last index to the first, indexes of subsequent elements to be processed are not modified even when element handled in current iteration is removed    
			for (var i = vacancies.length - 1; i >= 0; i--) {
				
				// Get a reference to object at index "i" of the array
				var currentVac = vacancies[i]; 
				
				// Concatenate values for vacancy-title, job-ref-number and employer name in that order seperated by a space
				var searchTarget = (currentVac.joPosition + ' ' + currentVac.joCode + ' ' + currentVac.joEmployerName).toLowerCase();
				
				// See if keyword is found in searchTarget
				var index = searchTarget.indexOf(keyword);	
				
				// If index < 0 (e.g. -1), indicates that the keyword was not found in searchTarget
				if (index < 0) {
					// If so, remove the element from the array
					vacancies.splice(i, 1);
				}
			}
		
		} 
		
		return vacancies; 
	}
	
	/**
	 * This function filters vacancies on the array accpeted for "vacancies" parameter, based on value in "location" parameter 
	 * 
	 * This searches location array in each element in "vacancies" array for value of "location" parameter and removes any element from "vacancies" that does not match. 
	 *
	 * @param vacancies: An array containing vacancy-objects that is searched through to find matches
	 * @param location: Value to search by in "vacancies" array
	 * 
	 * @return An array of vacancy-objects representing the search result
	 */
	function filterByLocation(vacancies, location) {
		// Convert keyword into lowercase
		location = location.toLowerCase();
		
		// If location == 'All Locations', it will be treated as an empty value
		if (location === 'all locations') { 
			location = '';
		}	

		// If location is not empty
		if (location.length > 0) {			
			// Loop through array
			// Iterating in reverse order due to objects' indexes being modified as matching elements get removed
			// When looping from last index to the first, indexes of subsequent elements to be processed are not modified even when element handled in current iteration is removed    
			for (var i = vacancies.length - 1; i >= 0; i--) {
				// Get a reference to object at index "i" of the array
				var currentVac = vacancies[i];
				// Get a reference to array in currentVac obj that is holding the set of location names for this vacancy 
				var vacLocations = currentVac.jobLocationsArray;
				// Initialise a boolean flag to be used to check if at least one element in vacLocations matches "location"
				var match = false;
				
				// Loop vacLocations
				$.each(vacLocations, function (locIndex, currentLocation) {
					// Check if element in vacLocations is an exact match with "location"
					if (currentLocation.toLowerCase() === location) {						
						match = true; // If so, assign true to flag						
						return false; // Terminate $.each(..) loop
					}
				});	
				
				// Check if there has been no match 
				if (!match) {
					// If no match, remove element from array
					vacancies.splice(i, 1);
				}
			}
		} 
		
		return vacancies;
	}

	/**
	 * This function controls which filtering function to call between DOM-based search function and array-based search function 
	 * 
	 * If the array accepted for "vacancies" parameter is present, that is taken as meaning that only part of the full-vacancy-collection is currently printed on the page. 
	 * This causes filterByKeyword(), filterByLocation() and loadMoreVacancies() functions to be called to filter-out non-matching elements from the the full set of vacancies, 
	 * making what is left the search result. A window-scoped variable, window.searchResult, is then updated by assigning this search result to it.    
	 * 
	 * @param: vacancies - Array of vacancy-objects on which filtering to be carried out
	 */
	function filter(vacancies) {		
		if (vacancies == undefined || vacancies == null) { // Check if vacancies are absent
			// if yes, indicates vacancies were not delivered in the form of an array; likely because full list of vacancies to display did not exceed the imposed vacancy-limit  
			filterVacancies();
		} else {
			// If no, it means vacancy-array is present in window scope; this indicates full list of vacancies to show 
			// did exceed imposed vacancy-limit and inifinity scrolling function is in effect

			// Make a deep copy (seperate objects) of window.vacancyCollection and assign to window.searchResult
			var searchResult = JSON.parse(JSON.stringify(vacancies)); 

			var keyword = $('.live-search-box').val(); // Retrieve current value in keyword-filter-box	
			searchResult = filterByKeyword(searchResult, keyword); // Execute search based-on keyword 

			var location = $('input.location-search-box').val(); // Retrieve current value in location-search-box
			searchResult = filterByLocation(searchResult, location); // Execute search based-on location 
			
			// create a clone of the vacTile before clearing out the DOM content
			if(window.vacTileDesign === undefined || window.vacTileDesign === null){	// check previously created vacTile design availabe 
				// Get a copy of the first vac-tile in the page, this will be used when creating vac-tiles next time
				window.vacTileDesign = $('div#job-ads').find('div.vbfa-screen.job-wrapper').find('div.row').children('div.job-ad.live-search-list')[0];
			}
			
			// Remove all existing vac-tiles from the vac-tile-container element in the DOM
			$('#job-ads').children('div.vbfa-screen.job-wrapper').children('div.row').children('div.job-ad.live-search-list').remove();

			// Update "window.searchResult" with "searchResult" 
			window.searchResult = searchResult;
			
			// Print the first batch of vacancies in searchResult
			loadMoreVacancies(searchResult);		
		}
		
		
		//color rows for searched vacancies. CC4732
		displayShadeRow();

		// Now that a new vacancy-set is present in the page (regardless of which search function was called), update location-drop-down
		// list of location-search-box
		constructLocationDropdownList();
	}
	/**
	 * Returns a string consisting of the HTML mark-up of vac-tiles for a given array containing vacancy-objects in individual elements
	 *
	 * @param an array containing vacancy-objects that an HTML string for vac-tiles is needed
	 *
	 * @return a string consisting of the HTML mark-up of vac-tiles to be printed for the collection of vacancy-objects in 
	 * vacancyCollection parameter
	 */
	function getVacancyHtml(vacancyCollection, firstIndex) {

		var newVacTileArray = [];	// array to hold newly created vacTiles
				
		// Loop through indexes of vacancyCollection array that should be printed on page
		for (var i = 0; i < vacancyCollection.length; i++) {
			
			var currentVacancy = vacancyCollection[i];
			
			// Remove leading zeros of job-ref-number (to be consistent with how job-ref-numbers are printed by code in JSP)
			var jobRefNumber = currentVacancy.joCode.replace(/^0+/, '');			
			
			var indexText = "jobAd" + (firstIndex + i);
			
			// Get a clone of the first vac-tile
			var newVacTile = $(window.vacTileDesign).clone();		// get a clone of a vacTile element
			
			// Set values to the container element of the cloned vac-tile
			var vacTileContainer = newVacTile;		// assign cloned vacTile to new vacTile element
			vacTileContainer.show();				// it is possible that the cloned vacTile might have hidden styles (when filters are selected or live search), so change styles
			vacTileContainer.attr('id', indexText);	
			vacTileContainer.attr('data-search-term',  currentVacancy.joPosition + ' ' + currentVacancy.joCode + ' ' + currentVacancy.joEmployerName);	
			var jobHrefLink = 	 '/vacancy?ac='+currentVacancy.agentCode+'&jc='+currentVacancy.joCode+'&ec='+currentVacancy.empCode+'&index='+(firstIndex+i)+'&rid=0&pg=applicant/vacancyDetails.jsp';// href to open standalone-adview
			// Set values to the vacancy-link of the cloned vac-tile
			var vacancyLink = newVacTile.find('a.openAd.job-link').attr('id', currentVacancy.joCode);	
			var endDate = newVacTile.find('span.closing-date');
			
			// Clear remaining dates value from closing date label in the cloned vac-tile
			vacTileContainer.find('span.closing-date').text('');
			
			vacancyLink.attr('id', currentVacancy.joCode);	
			vacancyLink.attr('data-empcode', currentVacancy.empCode);	
			vacancyLink.attr('data-agentcode', currentVacancy.agentCode);	
			vacancyLink.attr('data-index', indexText);	
			vacancyLink.attr('data-original-title', currentVacancy.joPosition);	
			vacancyLink.attr('data-title', currentVacancy.joPosition);
			// setting the starting date and closing date data attributes
			endDate.attr('data-startingdate', currentVacancy.startDate);	
			endDate.attr('data-closingdate', currentVacancy.expiryDate);	
			
			vacancyLink.attr('title', currentVacancy.joPosition);	
			vacancyLink.attr('href', jobHrefLink); 
			vacancyLink.attr('target', '_blank');  // open a vacancy in sepsrate tab
			vacancyLink.text(currentVacancy.joPosition);	
			
			offTouchJobLink(); // calling offTouchJobLink() to disable the clickability of the job position and company name 
			if('ontouchstart' in window)//ontouchstart - The event occurs when a finger is placed on a touch screen
			{
			var job_a_Tag = document.createElement('a'); // creating 'a' tag
			job_a_Tag.setAttribute('href', jobHrefLink); // attaching attribute href and its value to a created 'a' tag
			job_a_Tag.setAttribute('target', '_blank'); // set href to open using new browser tab
			
			var jobContent = newVacTile.find('div.job-content'); // find the most outer div of a vactile(job-content) 
			jobContent.wrap(job_a_Tag); // wrap() : wrap the job content div from 'a' tag created with href and target attributes. Enabling to click entire vactile
			}
			
			vacTileContainer.find('span.closing-date').text('');
			
			// Set values to job owner label in the cloned vac-tile
			var jobOwnerLbl = vacTileContainer.find('label.lbl-job-owner');		// get the label section
			jobOwnerLbl.attr('data-original-title', currentVacancy.joEmployerName);
			jobOwnerLbl.attr('data-title', currentVacancy.joEmployerName);	
			jobOwnerLbl.attr('title', currentVacancy.joEmployerName);	
			
			var ownerName = jobOwnerLbl.find('a.job-owner') || jobOwnerLbl.find('a.job-owner.no-link'); 	// the job owner label can have disabled status 
			ownerName.text(currentVacancy.joEmployerName); 		// set job owner name
			
			/*
			 * Check whether the vacancy is a TopAd vacancy or a featured employer vacancy with or without a company url 
			 * If topad/ featured with empty url value : disable link to company website, add class 'no-link', remove href and taget attributes. 
			 * Else, featured: enable the link, add 'http://' and create the full url and set value to attribut href, add target attribute to open website in a blank tab,
			 * 			remove class 'no-link'
			 */
			if ( (( currentVacancy.agentCode === 'DEFZZZ' ) || ( currentVacancy.employerUrl === '')) 	// check a topad vacancy or an empty website url
					?  ( ownerName.attr('disabled', 'disabled') && ownerName.removeAttr("href") && ownerName.addClass('no-link') && ownerName.removeAttr("target"))		// if true, TopAd or company with empty url
					: ( ownerName.attr('disabled', 'enabled')) && ownerName.attr('href' , 'http://' + currentVacancy.employerUrl) && ownerName.removeClass('no-link') && ownerName.attr('target', '_blank'));	// else, create a link to company web site
																																										
			

			// Set the job-ref-number in the cloned vac-tile
			newVacTile.find('span.job-ref-value').text(jobRefNumber);	
			
			newVacTile.find('label.job-location').remove();		// remove location section of the cloned vacTile			
			
			// Set job location(s)
			if (currentVacancy.jobLocationsArray != undefined && currentVacancy.jobLocationsArray != null && currentVacancy.jobLocationsArray.length > 0 && currentVacancy.jobLocationsArray != "") {
				
				// set locations of the vacancy
				setLocation(currentVacancy.jobLocationsArray, newVacTile);
			}	
								
			
			
			
			// Push the vac-tile clone into array
			newVacTileArray.push(newVacTile);		
		}		
		console.log('New vac-tile-batch created. size: ' + newVacTileArray.length);
		
		return newVacTileArray;
	}
	
	/**
	* Set vacancy locations of the vacTile. This will create a main location section if only a one location is available. 
	* Else, display the main location (which is the first location name of the location array) and create a tooltip for 
	* all sub locations
	
	* @param locationArray - location name array
	* @param vacTile - the current vacTile that needs to add the locations
	*/
	function setLocation(locationArray, vacTile){
		
		// Create label to display main location
		var mainLocation = '<label class="job-location" data-toggle="tooltip" data-placement="bottom" data-original-title="" data-title="" title="">&nbsp;<span class="location-area single-location"></span></label>';
		
		// Create label to display main location with a tooltip for sublocations	
		var subLocations = '<label class="job-location"><span class="plus-mark">+</span> <span class="location-area"></span> <span class="sub-location-tooltip">&nbsp;<span class="sub-location"></span></span></label>';
		
		var mainJobLocation = locationArray[0]; 	// main location name
		
		if (mainJobLocation != undefined && mainJobLocation != null && mainJobLocation.trim().length > 0) {		// locations are available for the vacancy		
 			if (locationArray.length > 1) {	// sub locations available
				
				$(vacTile).find('span.job-ref-value').after(subLocations);		// add the sub location section to the vacTile
				$(vacTile).find('label.job-location').find('span.location-area').text(mainJobLocation);		// set main location name
				
				var subLocElement = $(vacTile).find('span.sub-location-tooltip').html();		// get a single element where the sub location name should be added in the tooltip
				
				$(vacTile).find('span.sub-location').text(mainJobLocation);		// set the main location name as the first location value of sub location 

				$(vacTile).find('span.sub-location-tooltip').append('<br>');	// add a break after the first location name
				
				$.each(locationArray, function(idx, location) {		// iterate the sub location set except the main location name
					if (location != undefined && location != null && location.trim().length > 0 && idx !=0 ) {		// escape the first location name as it is already added to the sub location tooltip above

						$(vacTile).find('span.sub-location-tooltip').append(subLocElement); // append a new sub location name element to the vacTile
						$(vacTile).find('span.sub-location-tooltip span.sub-location:last-child').text(location);		// update the last sub location element of the tooltip
				
						if (idx != locationArray.length) {		// insert a line break
							$(vacTile).find('span.sub-location-tooltip').append('<br>');
						}
					}
				});

			} else {	// only the main location 
				$(vacTile).find('span.job-ref-value').after(mainLocation);			// add a main location section to the vacTile
			
				$(vacTile).find('label.job-location').attr('data-original-title', mainJobLocation);
				$(vacTile).find('label.job-location').attr('data-title', mainJobLocation);
				$(vacTile).find('label.job-location').attr('title', mainJobLocation);
				$(vacTile).find('label.job-location').find('span.location-area.single-location').text(mainJobLocation);
				
			}
			
		}
		
	}
	/* vacancy title tooltip on mouse hover */
	function initVacTileTooltips(){
		if(!('ontouchstart' in window))//ontouchstart - The event occurs when a finger is placed on a touch screen
		{
		//activates the bootstrap tooltip by initialising with the jquery tooltip() widget (jq-ui).
		$('body').tooltip({
	        selector: '[data-toggle="tooltip"]',
	        trigger: 'hover',
	        container: 'body'
	    }).on('mouseleave click' ,function () {
	        $('[data-toggle="tooltip"]').tooltip('hide');//hide the tooltip on mouse leave and onclick events
	    }); 
		// start search through the job-location div 
	   	$('.job-content').each(function(){ // select div in .job-content block
	   		var vacJobTitle = $(this).find('.job-title').text(); 										// Retrieves the text from each .job-title element
			var vacJobOwner = $(this).find('.job-owner').text();										// Retrieves the text from each .job-owner element
 			var vacJobLocation = $(this).find('.job-location .location-area').text();					// Retrieves the text from each .job-location element
 						   
				$(this).find('.job-title').attr({"data-toggle": "tooltip", "data-placement": "top", "data-original-title": vacJobTitle, "data-title": vacJobTitle, "title": vacJobTitle});				
                $(this).find('.lbl-job-owner').attr({"data-toggle": "tooltip", "data-placement": "bottom", "data-original-title": vacJobOwner, "data-title": vacJobOwner, "title": vacJobOwner }); //	Assigning tooltip for shortened .job-owner text to view the complete text on mouse hover
				
 				if($(this).find('.location-area').hasClass("single-location")){
 					$(this).find('.job-location').attr({"data-toggle": "tooltip", "data-placement": "bottom", "data-original-title": vacJobLocation, "data-title": vacJobLocation, "title": vacJobLocation}); //display tooltip for job location 
 				}
 			
	   	});		
	}else{
		$(this).find('.job-owner').removeAttr("href"); 
       	$(this).find('.job-owner').addClass("job-owner no-link"); 
	}
}
	function isTouchDevice(){
		if(!('ontouchstart' in window)){
			return false;
		}else
			return true;
	}
	/** 
	 * This function sets the vacancy-count shown next to functional area title in VBFA. 
	 * 
	 * If parameter "vacancies" is present, that is taken to mean that infinite-scrolling is in effect; the length of array accepted for "searchResult" 
	 * parameter is shown as job-count. 
	 * Else, shows the count of the currently visible vacancies.
	 *
	 * @param: vacancies - The full array of vacancy-objects which is checked to see if infinite scrolling is in effect
	 * @param: searchResult - Array of vacancy-objects whose count is set as the vacancy-count
	 *
	 */
	function displayJobCount(vacancies, searchResult) {
		var jCount = 0;
		// If "vacancies" is present, it indicates infinite scrolling is in effect
		if (vacancies != undefined && vacancies != null) {
			jCount = searchResult.length; // Get vacancy-count via searchResult
		} else { // If not, indicates infinite scrolling is not in effect; get count of visible vac-tiles
			jCount = $('.vbfa-screen').find(".job-content:visible").length; // add jCount to number of display vacancies 
		}

		$(".job-count").text(jCount); // set vacancy jCount value to the job-count span 

		if (jCount == 0) { // check jCount value if equal to zero 
			$(".empty-msg").show(); // if jCount value is zero, display 'No Vacancies' message 
		} else {
			$(".empty-msg").hide(); // if jCount value is not equal to zero, hide 'No Vacancies' message
		}
	}
	/* End job count and message display function */
		
    /**
 	* Sets the label for vacancy related dates including vacancy
 	* - start date
 	* - close date
 	* - number of remaining days if more than 24hrs remaining else display 'today'
 	* The span class is 'closing-date'. The data attributes 'closingdate' and 'startingdate' carries
 	* the closing date and the start date of the vacancy respectively. 
 	* This methods labels the closing date with a 
 	* user-friendly narration.
 	* It adjusts all the time calculations for UTC offsets to account for time-zone differences.
 	*
 	* @param vacancies: A JQuery array of DOM elements each having the attribute "data-closingdate" and a value representing 
 	* the closing-date of the vacancy (in format: yyyy-mm-dd) as value for that attribute. The narration of the closing date 
 	* prepared for each element in this array will be set as text of that element.     
 	*/    
 	function setDateLabel(vacancies) {
 		 
 		var ONE_DAY = 1000*60*60*24;		// seconds * minutes * hours * day
 		var MIN_TO_MILLIS = 60 * 1000;	// minutes to milliseconds, for adjusting UTC offsets
 		var LK_OFFSET = -330; 			// UTC is 330 (5.5H) minutes behind Sri Lanka
 		
 		/* label constants */
 		var IN_24H = "today";
 		var SOON = "soon";
 		var MANY_DAY_SUFFIX = "d";
 		var DATE_LABEL_TOOLTIP = "open date - close date (days to close)";
 		var timeNow = Date.now();	// todays date (in ms, UTC)
 		var theLabel = "";			// the closing date label to be displayed
 		var theSuffix = ""			// whats is displayed after the label e.g. 'days'
 		 /* traverse the closing date class in DOM */ 
 		 
 		// Resolve which attribute of the element to set the tool-tip content to; default is title attribute of the element (so the content set to it will be rendered as the 
 		// browser's default tool-tip)
 		 var attribToSetTooltip = 'title';		
			
		// If current UA is a Mircrosoft browser
		if(window.IS_IE_OR_EDGE){ 
			// Set the 'data-tooltip-content' as the attrib to set the tool-tip content to. This will prevent this content from being rendered as the browser's default tool-tip
			// This data-attribute is used in vbfa.css to construct a custom tool-tip on the fly; see selector 
			attribToSetTooltip = 'data-tooltip-content';
		}

		 $(vacancies).each(function(index) { 

 	 		  var timeNowTemp = timeNow;	// todays date (in ms, UTC)
 			  var labelPrefix = '+';	// get the existing prefix text in the span (before setting label.  Usu: Closing:)
 			  var closingDate = new Date($(this).data('closingdate')); 			// closing date (yyyy-mm-dd e.g. 2017-12-31 00:00 )
 			  var closingMillis = closingDate.getTime();  						// always UTC time
 			  closingMillis += LK_OFFSET * MIN_TO_MILLIS; 	// adjust UTC with offset.  the user at UTC + 0 has 5.5H less than the user in LK
 			  closingMillis += ONE_DAY - 1;  // add the remainder of the day.  i..e from midnight + 24 hours - 1 millisecond i.e 23:59:59.599 (closing date)
 			  dateNow = new Date(timeNowTemp);   // need a date object to calculate users UTC offset
 			  var utcOffset = dateNow.getTimezoneOffset();		// get the users UTC offset
 			 timeNowTemp += utcOffset * MIN_TO_MILLIS;				// and adjust the user time with the offset
 			  var millisBetween = closingMillis - timeNowTemp;		// duration between user's current time and closing date  		
 			  if (millisBetween > 0 && millisBetween <= ONE_DAY)
 			  	   theLabel = IN_24H;		// Closing: Today
 			  else if (millisBetween > ONE_DAY ) {		// more than a one day
 			  	   var daysBetween = Math.floor(millisBetween/ONE_DAY);			// e.g 2.5 days becomes 2.  better to floor and be safe.
 			  	   theLabel = labelPrefix + daysBetween + MANY_DAY_SUFFIX;     	// Closing: (+10d)   
 			  }  else if (millisBetween <= 0)
				   theLabel = SOON;												// Closing: Soon - for the user in a forward time zone e.g. australia 
 			  
 			  var cDate = $(this).data('closingdate');		// read closing date from data attributes
 			  var sDate = $(this).data('startingdate');		// read start date from data attributes
 			
 			  var cYear = cDate.slice(0,4);	// read vacancy closing date year
 			  var cMonth = cDate.slice(5,7);	// read vacancy closing date month
 			  var cDay = cDate.slice(8);		// read vacancy closing date day
 			  var sYear = sDate.slice(0,4);		// read vacancy start date year
 			  var sMonth = sDate.slice(5,7);	// read vacancy start date month
 			  var sDay = sDate.slice(8);	  	// read vacancy start date day
 			  
 			  var dateClosing = new Date(cYear, cMonth-1, cDay);	// create javascript date using closing date details
 			  var dateStarting = new Date(sYear, sMonth-1, sDay);	// create javascript date using start date details
 			  
 			  var monthArray = ['Jan', 'Feb', 'Mar', 'Apr', 'May', 'Jun', 'Jul', 'Aug', 'Sep', 'Oct', 'Nov', 'Dec'];
 			  
              
               var startDate = 	dateStarting.getDate() + " " + monthArray[dateStarting.getMonth()];
               var closeDate = dateClosing.getDate() + " " + monthArray[dateClosing.getMonth()];
               
               var dateLabel = '<span class="start-closing-label">' + startDate +' - ' + closeDate + '</span>';
               //<span class="days-remaining-label">(' + theLabel + ')</span>' ;
              $(this).append( dateLabel ) ;		// set the text
              
              $(this).attr(attribToSetTooltip, DATE_LABEL_TOOLTIP );//remove time zone details
 			});
 	 }  

	/**
		* 20171119 MM 784-4523 (adapted from openTiledView() in vacancybyfunctionalarea.jsp by SW)
		* 20171120 SW 784-4523 used vanilla js, with a loop. kiss.
		
		* Accepts the current page URL, extracts the querystring that declare the FA displayed
		* and prepares a matching URL to list VBFA, which is then displayed into the UA
		* by setting the href of the clicked anchor.
		* 
		* Note: the current page URL must have qstring with FA code simply because it is a vbfa.
		* So even if user edits the qstring from UA address bar, the page url taken from window.location.href has the original
		* URL with the qstring.  
		* 
		* param: pageURL - current page URL, something like: http://localhost:8080/do.landing?CO=FA&FA=SDQ
		* param: switchControl - anchor DOM element; what user clicked on to switch views
	*/
	function openListView(pageURL, switchControl){
		try { 				
			var listViewURL = "/applicant/vacancybyfunctionalarea.jsp?";		// not using full URI scheme.  Its OK. notice I appended the qstring terminator as its mandatory for VBFA. 
			var tokenQstr = pageURL.split("?");		// tokenise on qstring constant		
			var COMMAND_CODE = "CO";
			var DELIMITER = "&";
			var SWITCH_PARAM = "SV=y"
			if (tokenQstr.length > 0) {
				var params = tokenQstr[1].split(DELIMITER); // Tokenise parameters in query string on param delineator 
				/* loop through params and recreate qstring omitting only the command code
				** split: 0 is the key; 1 is the value; but dont need 1 as key=value format is available as param.
				** the extra & is removed after the loop. it reads nicer. */
				for (var i=0;i<params.length;i++) 
					if ((params[i].split("="))[0] != COMMAND_CODE)
						listViewURL += params[i] + DELIMITER; // split param into key/value
			}			
			// Check if there is no DELIMITER at the end of listViewURL
			if (listViewURL.lastIndexOf(DELIMITER) != listViewURL.length - DELIMITER.length) {
				listViewURL += DELIMITER; // append DELIMITTER 	
			} 

			listViewURL += SWITCH_PARAM; // append SWITCH_PARAM

			$(switchControl).attr('href', listViewURL); // update href value			
		} catch (error) {
			console.log('openListView() Exception : ' + error.name + '\n' + ' Error message : ' + error.message);
		}
	}
	
	/**
	 * Identifies how many vacancies are currently on the page and prints the next batch of vacancies from the 
	 * array of vacancy-objects accepted for "vacancies" parameter. 
	 *
	 * @param: vacancies - Array of vacancy objects from which the next batch should be printed
	 */
	function loadMoreVacancies(vacancies){
		
		// Get the number of vac-tiles currently in page; 
		// DIVs with class ".live-search-list" are container elements for each vac-tile and the length of their collection represents the total num of vac-tiles in the page
		var count = $('.live-search-list').length;
				
		// Check if "vacancies" is undefined or null 
		if (vacancies != undefined && vacancies != null && vacancies.length > 0) {
			
			// Check if full num of vacancies to be displayed in VBFA (which is available in "vacancies" array) is greater than what is currently displayed
			if (vacancies.length > count) { // If yes, it means more vacancies are there waiting to be printed
				
				// create a clone of the vacTile 
				if(window.vacTileDesign === undefined || window.vacTileDesign === null){	// check previously created vacTile design availabe 
					// Get a copy of the first vac-tile in the page, this will be used when creating vac-tiles next time
					window.vacTileDesign = $('div#job-ads').find('div.vbfa-screen.job-wrapper').find('div.row').children('div.job-ad.live-search-list')[0];
				}
				
				// Paint the next batch of vacancies...							
			
				// Get how many vacancies from the vacancies array should be printed at one time (vacancyLimit); this is set by JSTL
				// #job-ads is the container element for all of the vac-tiles in the page. In vacancyDetails.jsp the vacancyLimit value from DB is set as a data-attribute 
				// of this element to be accessible by scripts here
				var vacancyLimit = $('#job-ads').attr('data-vacancy-limit');
				
				// If vacancyLimit is available, and that value is a number
				if (vacancyLimit != undefined && vacancyLimit != null && $.isNumeric(vacancyLimit)) {

					var index = count;
					
					// The index in vacancies array up to which vacancies should be printed
					var endIndex = index + parseInt(vacancyLimit);	
					
					var jobsToPrint = vacancies.slice(index, endIndex);
					
					// Get the index of the first vacancy to print in the next batch of vacancies
					var firstIndex = index + 1;
					
					// Get a string of mark-up of vac-tiles to be printed on page 
					var htmlString = getVacancyHtml(jobsToPrint, firstIndex);
					
					// Create DOM elements for the vacancies being newly-inserted 
					if (count < 1) { // Check if there are currently any vac-tiles in the page 
						// True means there are no vac-tiles, place vac-tile mark-up as childern of the vac-tile container
						$('#job-ads').children('div.vbfa-screen.job-wrapper').children('div.row').append(htmlString);
					} else {
						// False means there are existing va-tiles; insert the new set after the last existing vac-tile element
						$('#job-ads').children('div.vbfa-screen.job-wrapper').children('div.row').children('div.job-ad.live-search-list').last().after(htmlString);
					}
					
					
					//color rows for the next batch of vacancies. CC4732
					displayShadeRow();
					
					// A batch of new vac-tiles were just created in DOM; now get those exact DOM elements
					var nextBatch = $('.live-search-list').slice(count, endIndex);
					
					// Set the 'Closing in' value for the newly printed vacancies
					setDateLabel(nextBatch.find('.closing-date'));
					
					// Set event handlers for job-links in vactiles that were just included in DOM  
					setJobLinkClickEventHandler(nextBatch);
				}
			}			
		}

		// Retrieve vacancy collection in window scope; window.vacancyCollection is declared & initialised by code in vacancyDetails.jsp
		var vacancies = window.vacancyCollection;

		// Retrieve whatever the content currently in window.searchResult 
		var searchResult = window.searchResult;		

		// Update the job-count displayed on VBFA to match the number now shown
		displayJobCount(vacancies, searchResult);		
	}
	
	
</script>

</head>
<body  onload="initBanners(); rotateBanners();">	<script language="JavaScript">
	
	var bannerList = new Array(0);		// array of banners for rotation
	var bannerCount = 0;					// number of banners
	var bannerIter = 0;										// banner iterator
	var bannerUrlList = new Array(0);		// array of banners for rotation
	
	/* **************************************************************************************************** *
	** Function to initialise array of banners for rotation                                                 *
	** It writes static array initialisation into this initBanners() function.                              *
	** example: bannerlist[0] = http://www.topjobs.lk/com/genesiis/sdb/banner/....{path to banner}          *
	** This is done on the server side.                                                                     *
	** When the script is executed on the client the array is used to rotate banners.                       *
	** **************************************************************************************************** */
	
	function initBanners() {
		
		// console.log("init banner function");		// DEBUG
		
		// loop on the list of banners from the servlet view and populate the js array
		
		// list on the console for DEBUG only
		// for(var i=0;i<bannerCount;i++) {console.log(bannerList[i]);}
	}

	/* ************************************************************************************** *
	** Function to rotate banners							                                  *
	** sets the image source to value of banner array element.  timeout set to call function  *
	** repetitively.																		  *
	** TODO: handling default banner, banner randomising, specific duration					  *
	** ************************************************************************************** */

	function rotateBanners(){
		// console.log("rotate banner function;bannercount="+bannerCount+";bannerIter="+bannerIter);		// DEBUG
		if (bannerCount > 0) {
			var currentIndex = bannerIter % bannerCount;  // Calculate index once to keep image and URL in sync
			document.getElementById("TRB").src = bannerList[currentIndex];
			document.getElementById("bannerUrl").href = bannerUrlList[currentIndex];
			bannerIter++;  // Increment only once after using the index
			window.setTimeout("rotateBanners()", 5000);
		}
	}
</script>
